Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
37
Compilation Committee for Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Current Position of the Unification Church
Up until now, the personal crosses in your families may have been lifted as the Unification Church has progressed. However, the cross that the teacher of the Unification Church is carrying has not yet been lifted. 
The position of the teacher who used to guide you in the past regarding your individual circumstances is different from the position he holds today concerning society, the nation, and the world. So, which time is more serious? That time was serious, but this time is even more serious. 
The Reason for the Retreat of Members Despite the Church's Development
Today, the emotional stance of Unification Church members has changed significantly compared to that time. Although it seems that Unification Church members have changed and developed due to the different historical background, this has resulted in a gradual retreat rather than progressive development. Nevertheless, the Unification Church is making gradual progress. 
Why is that? It is because the teacher is in a more serious position than before. Back then, he worked with the nation and the people in mind for a distant future. He endured hardships while looking forward to a time when the opportunity for resolution and restoration would inevitably come. Now, that anticipated time has arrived. That time is not always present. 
When we look at the history of restoration up to now, has God ever chosen a central figure twice to work through? He chose Abraham twice, but the conditions were different. God chooses a central figure once, and if that figure misses the time and fails to fulfill their mission, He does not raise that person again to work through them a second or third time. Therefore, if the time is missed once, that is it. 
For this reason, you must have a deep interest in the time that is approaching. The current members of the Unification Church must have a more serious heart than those early members who faced persecution. They must fight from an absolute position that cannot be compromised. Because this standard remains, the Unification Church has developed through the teacher. It has not developed because of the Unification Church members. 
So, why is there such a difference? You are not standing in a serious position like the teacher. The teacher feels that he must comfort God in any hardship by becoming one with Him, but today you are appealing based on your own difficulties. You should be thinking more about God's difficulties and sympathizing with them, yet it is easy to forget God's hardships and stand in a position where you only wish to be comforted yourself. 
This will lead to destruction. Such people will find their paths blocked. 
The Nature of the Absolute
Dear friends, where does a true filial child come from? There may be those who have the foundation of inherited wealth from their parents and fulfill their duties and etiquette toward them in ordinary circumstances. However, there are also those who, without any inheritance or wealth, overcome difficult circumstances and devote all their efforts and sincerity to serve their parents as a filial child. 
When comparing those who fulfill their filial duties in an environment where everything is provided with those who carve out their own path in difficult circumstances, the difference is vast. 
In faith, the life that is spoken of is not formed through compromise between two parties or through relationships with the environment; it is formed from an absolute position. This is unavoidable. This absolute position is not a place that everyone can look at, dance, and be happy about. The absolute position is an extremely lonely place. There cannot be two in that position. There is only one. The absolute transcends relative conditions. That position is extremely difficult, extremely frustrating, extremely lonely, and if it is dangerous, it is extremely dangerous. 
What direction can the absolute take? There cannot be two directions. There is only one. Therefore, an absolute existence for good cannot retreat because of evil. It cannot go before evil. It is always an absolute existence in a good position. You must understand this. 
For this reason, the prophet Elijah also cried out to God on Mount Horeb, saying, "I alone am left." Even though all the people in society, including the priests, had gone to the Baal god, the only one standing for God was Elijah. That position is precious. The position of saying, "I am the only one." The position of saying, "There are many people on this earth, but the only one remaining before the Father is me." That is the absolute position. 
With this awareness of such a position, one must be determined to pave any difficult path to achieve the great work of new creation, so that one can stand in a position that corresponds to God's work of re-creation. Do you understand what I mean? God created the heavens and the earth from such a position. He began creating all things from a unique position. 
Fallen humans must go through the process of re-creation according to the principles of creation. Therefore, the question is how to make fallen humans aware of their independent standards. 
The absolute position is an extremely lonely place. Why is it lonely? It is lonely because humans have fallen and become evil. Why is it sad? It is sad because it is in an evil environment. That is the axis. 
Moreover, why is that position miserable? It is miserable because it is a good position that is just a dot in a world of evil. However, in that place, misery does not simply disappear as misery. When one overcomes that miserable environment and breaks through the lonely environment, new joy of goodness that can surpass loneliness arises. 
Where does the joy of goodness arise? When something good happens to you, you boast about it. For example, among students who scored only 10 points, if there is a student who scored 11 points, what will that student do? Will they boast or not? They will boast. Is 11 points the best? Anyone who thinks that is the best is crazy. 
In the same way, from God's perspective, there are many denominations and many believers who only score 10 points. But if someone says, "As a Unification Church member, I am better than that," can that be acceptable? The absolute standard is thousands of miles away, and if someone boasts that they are better, are they a good person or a bad person? From the perspective of the absolute standard, they are crazy in broad daylight. 
Also, if there is a person who scored 91 points among those who scored 90 points, will that person boast? Yes, they will boast. Of course, they are slightly better than others, but from the absolute standard, that person is also crazy. They are just a little less crazy, existing in a neurotic phenomenon. Furthermore, when looking at 100 points, can 99.999, no matter how many nines you add, ever compare to 100 points? It cannot compare to 100 points. The difference may seem negligible. To the eye, there is no difference. 
Is the blinking of my eyes the same as the blinking of your eyes? Yes, it is. However, in terms of content, it is not the same. It is absolutely different. Therefore, the nature of the absolute must be unique, unchanging, and eternal. 
Absolute Life
Is life absolute or relative? "It is absolute." It wants to be absolute. Everyone wants to be absolute. Why is that? Because it is a necessary existence before the absolute being, it is considered absolute. Do you understand what I mean?
If there is an absolute element in my life, then the absolute being will regard it as absolute. The absolute exists because there is something relative. 
So why do we try to regard life as absolute? It is because God delights in placing my life in a relative position. Without that, God does not regard it as absolute.
No matter how absolute God is, He cannot move with one leg. No matter how much He tries to move with one leg, it remains as it is. But what would be good about that? Would you like to just sit alone and remain as you are? Can you be happy sitting alone saying, "Oh, I am a millionaire and I have so much money. Oh, how nice!"? Even if you feel good about it, there arises a desire for someone to share in that joy. 
The position of the absolute being is a lonely position. Even if there is joy in that position, the joy possessed inside and outside is not stimulating. God created the heavens and the earth to receive the stimulation of that joy.
We are in the relative position of the absolute being, and even though the absolute being stands in our relative position, why does He regard us as absolute? It is because He can find joy in us. There, conversations can happen, laughter can occur, and exchanges can take place. When alone, that cannot happen. If one is sitting quietly alone, one cannot know whether something good exists or not. However, when there is mutual exchange, one can then understand what is good. 
Therefore, we can understand that the absolute being places us in a position of being regarded as absolute to find joy. To find joy... Creation began from here. 
So, what do we find joy in? It is not in things we can touch with our hands. Have you ever touched a dove? When you catch and touch a dove, it feels soft and very tender. The more you touch it, the more affection you feel. Try catching and touching it; how does it feel? When you feel good touching it, is it only good because of your hands? What is good? Is it only the hand that feels good? Is it only the eyes that feel good? It is not just that; my whole body feels good. Therefore, eating, smelling, and seeing are all enjoyed by my whole body. 
While everything is good, what is the best among them? It is the counterpart. When I call out, "Hey!" the counterpart responds, "Yes." When I call out, "Hey!" they respond, "Uh-huh!" When a husband calls his beloved wife tenderly and softly, "Honey!" she responds tenderly and softly, "What is it?" But if he calls out brusquely, "Hey!" she responds, "What do you want?" Just like the sound of the mountains, everything is relative. 
So, what is the best? Is it food? That is not the best. While one eats and feels good, that is temporary. After eating to one's fill, one may refuse more food. 
However, when it comes to the person one loves, it is not the same. Is there anyone who says, "I will forget you. I don’t want you"? The more you see them, the more you want to see them. Isn’t that right? You want to see them again and again. Thus, they stand in front of you while you stand behind, rotating like a wheel. This is where unity occurs.
If we keep talking like this, when will we reach the current position? We are going back to the place where 6,000 years of history began, right? So let’s hurry up and talk, shall we? "Please take your time." You want to take your time? "Yes." If you miss breakfast, you will be hungry, right? "It’s the same after eating." It’s the same after eating? (Laughter) 
To stand in the position of God's counterpart, one must receive recognition for possessing absolute value. Why? Because that is how the principles of creation are set. So can the absolute being recognize a monkey, which is similar to a human, as an absolute being capable of standing in the position of God's counterpart? Can God say, "Oh, Monkey! Please come here"? Think about it. The dimensions are different. 
The Human Body is the Palace of Mystery
Science says, "Where is God? All beings have naturally evolved and developed. Creation cannot exist." Is that correct? The dimensions of monkeys and humans are different. Their cognitive faculties are different. 
Can there be dreams in the monkey world? Can there be concepts like ethics and morality? No, there cannot. The life of a monkey is one-dimensional. However, humans are three-dimensional. "Then how does the one-dimensional become three-dimensional?" If you ask, they will say, "It adapts." Adaptation is good, but it is because God created it that way. 
Now, let me ask you one thing. Have you seen God? Raise your hand if you haven’t seen Him. God can always be recognized. Would you like to know how? "Yes." 
What do your eyes look like? They are black, right? These eyes blink and even wink; it’s quite amusing. Did these eyes say, "I will be born as eyes" when they were born, or did they just happen to be born as eyes? "They just happened to be born as eyes." Then, when these eyes were formed, did they know there was a sun? Did they know that when they were born, there would be a sun? "No, they didn’t." If they didn’t know, how could these eyes be formed to see the sun? "Because it is innate." Innate? 
When the eyes of the original ancestors, Adam and Eve, were formed, did they say, "I will just be born"?
"Did it come to be like this because it thought, 'I should come to be like this knowing there is a sun,' or did it just happen to come to be like this? This is a question we should think about. If the eye itself knew that there was a sun, it would have thought, 'I should come to be like this.' If you were to ask the eye, it would probably respond, 'I knew there was a sun when I was formed as an eye.'

Then, would the knowledge come before or after the sun? 'If it knew, it must come first.' It must come first. It means it was born knowing everything. The reason the eye is like this is because there was an existence that knew there was a sun when it came out.

Let’s think about the ear for a moment. Did the ear know that there was air on this earth when it was formed, or did it not know? 'It knew.' What made this ear come out like this? Because the air must not escape. It is designed to receive sound waves well in the air. So, it is a wonderful resonator. Would it have come to be like this as if it were a toy, saying, 'Hey ear, you should be like this'? It did not happen naturally. Is there anything that happens naturally? Can there be a result without a cause in this world?

So, when the ear itself came out as this resonator, did it know that there was air on this earth, or did it not know? 'It knew.' Even if the ear itself did not know, the essence knew such things. It did not all happen naturally. What if the ear were attached backward? Just think about it being flipped. It would not hear well. If that happened, it would be a big problem.

Now, let’s think about the nose. Did this nose know that it had to smell through the air when it was born on this earth, or did it not know? 'It knew.' It came out knowing everything, right? 'Yes.' But what if the nose were attached upside down? It would be a big problem on a rainy day, right? Just think about it. (laughter) So, how wonderfully designed is the nose? It is shaped like a trumpet, preventing rain while allowing for the sense of smell. When air comes in, the nose is well equipped to filter it. It is designed to not miss any impurities in the air.

Did it know better than you, or not? Is the nose better than you? 'It is better.'

Also, the mouth needs to eat well but also needs to speak. When you look at the lips, they move in perfect harmony when speaking. When you say to go up, it goes up simultaneously with thought, and when you say to go down, it goes down simultaneously with thought. But what would happen if you thought of speaking after thinking, and the mouth was closed? Could you speak? If you think, 'Hey!' and then the mouth is about to close but is open, would that work? The timing is perfectly synchronized with thought.

Looking at the tongue, it has some remarkable abilities. However, it looks quite plain. What use is a tongue that looks like a palm? Yet this tongue has extraordinary abilities in the universe. It was born knowing that it could speak like this. Can you speak without a tongue? In some cases, it can be long, in others flat, and in some round; it changes in various ways. When a person pronounces words, it can be blunt, smooth, abrupt, or sharp, all in its own way.

And then there are the teeth. This is very dangerous. Just think about how dangerous it is. The tongue is softer than a child's hand. But think about the tongue moving in and out between the teeth that are constantly clashing. How dangerous is that? The tongue probably feels like an atomic bomb is colliding right in front of it every time the teeth move. (laughter)

Yet, there are no accidents. While the teeth occasionally touch each other, there are times when the tip gets slightly bitten, but the tongue is never bitten off. How is it that they know each other so well and play together in harmony? Without even thinking, the tongue thinks, 'If I make a loud noise while speaking, it will be a big problem,' and when the teeth touch, it doesn't say, 'Be careful, be careful.' Yet, it all works out well. Moreover, this tongue was born knowing it had to eat. The teeth also knew they had to bite something to eat.

Even when looking at the hands, what if they bent backward instead of forward? Yet, they bend forward so that they can grab everything. Did the hand know that when it was formed, or did it not know? 'It knew.' It knew.

Thus, the human body is a palace of mysteries, a palace of mysteries. Whatever scientists or scholars say, it is all nonsense. If someone were to study just one finger and write a book, they could not write millions of books. The human body is a palace of mysteries. There are over 400 trillion cells in the human body, all moving and functioning differently. If you magnify this, it is larger than the universe.

This is a mysterious entity that can live a daily life, a yearly life, and a lifetime without any collisions, achieving harmony. Yet, scientists say it just adapts naturally and evolves naturally. Those kids...

How does one become two? To become two from one, there must be a force added here. Who adds that force? Does the entity itself generate force and develop? There is no such principle. Without a third force being added, it does not grow. Over time, force is consumed. In electricity, there is input and output. Is there a law where input and output become equal? If the electricity that is input is output, will that force grow or shrink? It absolutely shrinks.

How does evolution happen according to evolution theory? Evolution theory is the opposite of the law of input and output. Where is there such a principle in the world? Evolution theory is about absolute growth, right? 'It shrinks.' Does evolution shrink? 

According to evolution theory, the amoeba naturally arises, gradually grows into a monkey, and evolves into a human. According to evolution theory, does that mean it grows or shrinks? 'It grows.' However, in the principle of force, when input and output are equal, it cannot grow at all. It shrinks. There is a consumption of force.

From this perspective, force arises through action. Without action, force does not arise. Yet, do you deny this principle? Did force grow from something small? That line of reasoning must end now.

Therefore, if we look at ourselves, we were all born knowing everything from the beginning. Right? I did not know, but my father and mother knew. That is why they made the eyes and said, 'You must be like this because there is sunlight.'

How many layers does the eye have? It consists of the sclera, the iris, and the pupil. It fits perfectly into the stages of creation, growth, and completion. If you look at the nose, there are one or two holes, and they combine into one inside. It is a completion. The ear is also divided into three parts, and these combine to allow hearing. If you fold your fingers, you see one, two, three. If you look closely, they are all arranged in threes. Everything is orderly.

The eyes symbolize God and represent human character. When you look at your own face and think you are good-looking, you find the eyes fascinating. How fascinating they are, just look closely. The eyelids are like bars. Why were they made? Did they know this was necessary, or not? 'They knew.' Without them, the eyes would become a trash can. When the east wind blows, the west wind blows, the south wind blows, and the north wind blows, dust would all enter the eyes. That is why we have eyelashes. And by blinking, even if dust gets in, it cleans it out. If they were stiff and stayed still, what would happen? It would be a big problem. Did the eyelids know they had to clean? 'They knew.' They knew all of that.

What about the eyebrows? They are dark and thick, not just one but two, sticking to the forehead. You might think that is unpleasant, but if you think about it, you might feel, 'Wow, they are well placed.' They are there to remove unnecessary things while holding firm. Those hairs are necessary for us. If there were no eyebrows, where would the sweat go when it flows from the forehead? It would go straight into the eyes. Because of the eyebrows, it diverts away.

The eyes are slightly recessed, but the edges are exposed. Why is that? When tears flow, they are directed that way. They cannot flow this way at all. (demonstrating) Right? When you think about these things, you realize how mysterious our bodies are. So, as you look at this, you should praise, 'Even when God made the eyebrows, He made them with such marvelous skill.' So, are they useful or not? 'They are useful.' Who placed them there? Would someone say, 'This also occurred naturally'? Did the eyebrows occur naturally? They did not occur naturally.

Then, who arranged the eyes like this? What if the eyes were attached to the back of the head? Just think about it. So, you need to understand these things.

What is the neck for? It moves because of the eyes. The eyes symbolize God. When any creature is born, if you look closely, the eyes are the first to appear. Even when a frog hatches from an egg, the eyes are very large. The eyes come first. Isn’t that strange? Therefore, the eyes symbolize God.

The nose symbolizes Adam and Eve. The face symbolizes the universe. The nose in the center of the face symbolizes Adam and Eve. They say if the nose is well-shaped, one will live well. If the nose is poorly shaped, no matter how good-looking the face is, it will ruin it. If the nose is well-shaped, even if the face is ugly, it will be balanced. But when you see someone with a flat nose, you might think, 'Oh, how unfortunate.' A flat nose is considered unattractive. So, the nose must be well-shaped. If you keep looking at the teacher's nose, it might make you feel uncomfortable. (laughter)

How can you know a person's character? You can tell by looking at their eyes. You can tell right away. Character follows nature, so you can tell by looking at the eyes. If I were to choose someone among those here who is like a thief, I could pick them out immediately. In that respect, I am an expert. A physiognomist is just a guesser.

So, when I send you off to get married, I can help you meet good husbands or bad husbands. For those who have put in a lot of effort for a purpose, they will meet a good husband, while those who have not put in effort will meet a bad husband, even if they are good-looking. Shouldn’t it be that way? If their ancestors were good and their descendants were loyal for a purpose, they will meet a good husband. Do you oppose that? Do you young ladies oppose that?

When you think about these things, looking at faces is incredibly interesting. Now, let’s look at the head. It is covered with hair like a porcupine. However, it is very well covered. You cannot wrap it with a cloth... (laughter) The important parts are wrapped. The head is indeed an important part, isn’t it? Why is it that only the head is wrapped while other parts are exposed? Because it is a very important place.

You also have hair under your armpits, right? Do you know what that is? It is a pump. It is a pump that has a dispersing function. It is all necessary.

When you look at it, you can see that the limbs and body are all intricately arranged. This is designed by the greatest designer. So, when you look at the eyes, would you say God exists or not? 'I would say He exists.' There is no need to insist on it. We were all born knowing.

When a boy is born, does he know there is a girl? Did he know or not? 'He knew.' If he were born and was alone as a boy, wouldn’t that feel bad? And if a girl is born and finds herself alone, wouldn’t that feel bad? Isn’t that so? Therefore, when a girl is born, does she know there is a boy? Did she know or not? Although I did not know, the one who gave birth to me knew. The reason I was born a girl is that there is a boy who needs me. Likewise, the reason I was born a boy is that there is a girl who needs me. Isn’t that so? 'Yes.' We were all born knowing that.

So, when you look at that, does God exist or not? Think about whether God exists or not. You can know right away. Looking at the nose, there are nose hairs. If something is blocked in the pipe, wouldn’t that feel bad? If the pipe is blocked, it feels bad.

The principle pipe should be smooth so that air can flow out easily, but if something is blocking it, how unpleasant would that be? The nostrils should be clear, but why are they complicated with hairs? Look at the holes. You can’t see them even if you look upside down. If you haven’t seen it, look at your friend’s nostrils before eating. See if what I say is right or not. The hairs have blocked it well. All the hairs are directed toward the center, blocking it well. The air mainly goes in the middle, but dust must not enter, so the hairs are directed toward the center. Does that seem right, or not? Take a look. You are living without knowing that... (laughter) When you see this, you realize how mysterious our bodies are.

Hair is like a tree. If you grab the hair and rub it, you can tell where the root is and where the end is. It is like leaves, so you can tell. When you look at these things, you can see that everything is intricately made to protect the body.

When you look at it this way, it has been studied and determined through encyclopedias, designed, and made into a masterpiece with one hundred percent value. This is a person. Do you understand? But did a person just arise naturally? Those kids...

Do you know how precious fingernails are? How would you grab things without fingernails? To know how precious fingernails are, try pulling one off. You will realize how precious they are. And look at the palm and the back of the hand. The skin is shaped differently. When you look closely at each part, you can see how perfectly arranged and well-made they are; the more you look, the more mysterious it becomes. It is made so well that you cannot imagine anything beyond that. The very essence of it is mysterious.

Eternal love."
Let me ask you whether you believe in God or not. From a perspective unrelated to the Unification Church, do you think there is a creator who made you, or do you think there isn't? "I think there is." Even if you ask this to communists, they won't be able to respond.

If you tell a man, "You are not a man, you are a woman," he would say, "Why am I a woman? I am a man." If you then ask, "Really? Then why do men and women look different?" he wouldn't be able to answer. If you ask, "How can you say whether God exists or not when you don't even know this?" even communists would be at a loss for words. If you ask, "Why does the nose look like this? How can you know God without knowing that?" they would be speechless. It might be okay to approach the conversation this way.

Does God exist or not? If you say He doesn't, then life in this world becomes meaningless. Then what should the eyes see? The eyes should see good things. When watching a movie, do you want to watch a bad movie or a good movie? You want to watch a good movie. Do you go just to watch, or do you go to feel something? You go to watch a good movie and to be moved.

The ears also want to hear good things. They don't want to hear bad things. Why do we enjoy music if we want to hear bad things? You might as well go to the restroom and listen to the sound of a trumpet. (Laughter) So what kind of sound do you want to hear when enjoying music? You want to hear good sounds. Among good sounds, you want to hear the best sounds.

Therefore, you want to see the best things, hear the best things, smell the best things, and touch the best things. So what is the best of good things? It is love. And who is the master of love, the king of love? It is God, who created heaven and earth.

When a person reaches around 20 years of age, they go through puberty, and at that time, a man begins to understand what a woman is like. So he thinks about studying hard to find a wonderful lady to marry and to become a good father. Do you think like that or not? "I think so." Those who don't think like that should die. So if anyone raises their hand saying they want to marry a bad woman, there wouldn't be a single person. (Laughter) And if there are any women who would raise their hand saying they want to marry a bad husband, it would ruin their mood. There is no need to ask.

People want to feel good things in everything they eat, touch, etc. Humans are made to feel good through their sensory organs, right? They are made to feel good. So what is good? People talk about happiness, and that is people. Love is not just seeing someone you like once. The more you see them, the more you want to see them, and you want to see them forever. It is not something that is good temporarily and then bad. Love is eternal.

"Everlasting love!" they say, right? Is there a couple that says, "I will love you for just one year"? What would you prefer? It feels good to say you will love forever. Would someone who cannot live even a hundred years say, "I will love you for three hundred years"? If a husband says to his wife, "I will love you for three hundred years," what would her mood be like? Would she feel good or bad? Ladies, answer me! Would she feel good or bad? "Bad." (Laughter) If someone says they will love for three hundred years, would that be okay? It is true that they cannot live for three hundred years, but they don't want to hear such words. Therefore, love is broad and eternal.

So when you love eternally, is it good today and bad tomorrow? No. It becomes more and more three-dimensional. It becomes like a pyramid. It is also like a crystal. Even if a crystal breaks and turns to powder, it retains the same crystalline shape. Love is like the crystal structure. The more you attach it, the more it becomes like a pyramid. If we speak in terms of branches, the shape of a big branch and a small branch is the same. There are differences in size, but the shape and essence are the same.

To love God, who is the center of love, is where human happiness lies. Where is that good? Happiness does not come from just having good eyes, a good mouth, a good nose, good ears, or good touch. Happiness is not just in any of these senses alone; it is in the place where all these senses come together and can say, "Ah, this is good." When you reach such a place, you can experience all tastes: sour, salty, bitter, spicy, and sweet.

Everyone, there is something called the five flavors, right? What is the stimulating desire that you cannot help but want to feel, which allows you to experience the joy of those five flavors? That is love. Do you understand?

When you experience the spiritual world, you can feel such stimulation. Even if you don't eat, it is better than eating, and even if it is a dark night, it is better than daytime. There is nothing bad there.

If a couple, even if they only have a handful of barley rice that rolls around when blown, live happily while loving and laughing, would they be happy or unhappy? "Happy." They would be happy. Therefore, happiness comes from overcoming unhappiness. Happiness overcomes death.

So when you ask how long a couple will love each other, if they say they will love only until they are young, would that feel good or bad? "Bad." Until when do you want to love? "Forever!" They pray for "forever," but they wish to love until they die, and then love forever afterward. Eternity represents the future and replaces the whole. To say they will love until they die means they will give all of themselves to love. Right? "Forever" is total, and "until I die" means they will love completely. That is what feels good.

2)
The Limit of Restoration
God is in a pitiful position, needing to turn His heart and reach out to raise fallen humanity to a point of hope. Regardless of the historical process, God must intervene so that humanity can retain the original value of creation as it was intended. We must understand that there is infinite internal suffering for God in this matter.

Human beings, who can now call God "Father" as a result of sacrifice, have added countless times more sorrow to God than the sorrow He felt when He first dealt with humanity. As I reflect on the fact that I am born from such a lineage of ancestors, I must recognize that I have no content to stand confidently before God.

It goes without saying that we are in a position that is insufficient to stand before God, and we must be grateful that He thinks of us. When we consider this, we should understand the immense burden God carries to restore us as His sons and daughters, and further, as the princes and princesses of the heavenly kingdom.

Human beings tend to think of everything from a self-centered perspective. When they are sad, they believe the whole world is sad, and when they are happy, they think the world is happy too. God is the same. When God is happy, the world manifests as an object of joy; conversely, when God is sad, the world inevitably becomes an object of sorrow. Just as we humans are like this, God cannot be any different.

When we think about whether God has ever experienced a moment of joy in His historical relationship with humanity, it is clear that He has not. God has been fighting to overcome sorrow and desires a day of joy. This is the providential course that God has continued through our ancestors.

We must expand from the individual providential course to the family providential course, then to the tribal, national, and ultimately the global providential course, laying the foundation for victory on a worldwide scale. Furthermore, through this global victory, we must envision a foundation that can restore the universe to its original state of creation and establish sons and daughters whom God can eternally love. The path of God in this endeavor is an immense path of suffering, and we must recognize that it is a path of pain that cannot be ignored.

Despite God's heart in this matter, there may have been ancestors who caused Him greater sorrow and those who caused Him less. When we examine our ancestral history, it is undeniable that we have increased God's sorrow and left behind conditions of sorrow throughout our history. Additionally, as a living being, as an individual looking towards the future, we must recognize whether we are indeed in a position that can bring joy to God.

You stand on the victorious foundation that has been built upon the efforts of God over 6,000 years and the sacrifices of countless prophets and ancestors. You have been able to call God "Father" because you stand on this victorious foundation. You should sincerely thank God for being able to stand in such a glorious position.

How much have I changed from my past self to my present self?
There is a significant historical distance between my past self and my present self. This distance can correspond to over 6,000 years in the emotional world. The world until now has not been one of joy but rather one that has traversed through a history of sorrow and tragedy. Considering that this period of 6,000 years corresponds to thousands or millions of years in God's emotional world, there is a stark difference between my past self and my present self. 

How great is this difference? You must understand that there is a difference as vast as heaven and earth.

Now, when you look at yourself before and after entering the Unification Church, what has changed? When you examine your own position, it may seem that you are the same as before, with the same heart, but there is a world of difference in the content inside and out. You must recognize how much I have changed compared to my past self.

When comparing the value standards of my past self and my present self, I must feel that I stand on a value standard that cannot be exchanged for anything. The extent of this realization will determine whether your future lives can be guided in the right direction.

The journey from my past self to my present self has not been a smooth one. It has required an indescribable path of indemnity. This path has been one of overcoming, suffering, sorrow, and twists and turns.

Even if you have not experienced such twists and turns and suffering, historical tragedies and pains have intervened to bring about differences in your current value standards. It is important to understand how you handle that unfortunate history.

You should not lament the value gained through such experiences but rather have a heart of gratitude. You have received God's grace until now, but you must strive to ensure that God's unchanging grace and protective hand do not leave you in the future. The more you feel that your current value standard has risen compared to the past, the more you will desire to stand in a position that is significantly higher tomorrow than it is today. When that happens, you will be able to walk the rightful path of heaven.

You will be able to maintain a course that heads straight toward the standard of God's restoration providence. However, if you are unable to do so, it is an undeniable fact that you will encounter unexpected results due to the blurred direction of your heart.

What is the highest value standard that humanity pursues?
So where is the limit of the restoration path? This is the question. We humans do not want to remain within the limits of our individual value pursuits. We want to adapt beyond the limits of individual value to the environment, and not only to the environment but also to the nation, and further, to the world, seeking global values. In this light, the standard of value that humanity uses as a benchmark is one that approaches absolute goodness.

So where is the highest point of life that our hearts desire? If there is a Creator who created heaven and earth, we desire to reach a standard where we can meet that absolute being.

But does everything end when I meet the absolute being? No, it does not. We must pursue a position where we form an eternal relationship with the absolute being, a position that cannot be severed.

What must we do to achieve this? We must monopolize God's one and only love. It is only by monopolizing that love that the desires we pursue in life are finally fulfilled. Until we achieve that, there will always be a longing in our hearts, and thus the value of our individual humanity will remain incomplete.

So where can we meet the limit of human value completion and desire pursuit? It is not only by meeting the absolute God but also by conquering God's one and only love, so that that love is with me and can be claimed as my own, that human beings can finally fulfill their highest desires.

Dividing Good and Evil
Today, countless people on this earth live without knowing what the heart is. In other words, they do not realize that the heart itself is the foundation for forming my character centered on God's love. The heart is great. The heart is infinitely vast and tremendous. Within that heart, there is room to accommodate God. When anyone possesses a correct heart, they wish to transport all humanity to a palace of peace at once.

The direction and method of that heart give rise to the direction of good and the direction of evil. The purpose that is desired based on that foundation of the heart is immense, but the direction and method taken to achieve that purpose can vary, leading to different paths of good and evil.

Evil people are not much different from us. The methods they employ differ slightly from ours. They might argue, "I thought this way would help me achieve my goal faster, so I took that approach, but the purpose is the same." You can find many such people in prisons. Thus, the division between good and evil arises based on direction and method.

From now on, you must go through a path of struggle. As you enter a higher realm of competition, you must objectively examine your position from a third-party perspective, looking at yourself in the position of pursuing the standard of victory and the value of glory. The question then becomes, what path should I take, what course should I choose, and what direction should I pursue? You must understand this.

You must know how you are.
Today, you should reconsider the question of how you are. More than the question of what methods and directions you will take, you must first know how you are. You are not alone. You are two. You will know that your body and heart are fighting for different purposes. This is the issue.

My heart is me, and my body is clearly me, but there is a real "me" and a false "me." There is a "me" that is necessary for me and a "me" that is not necessary. What is this? One is the person of the heart, and the other is the person of the body. The direction the person of the heart goes is different from the direction the person of the body goes. You are standing at this boundary, deciding which person to follow, and you are on the path of destiny that must choose one direction. This is the path that fallen humanity must take. This path is one that cannot be denied, as it is a process that must be walked daily, whether one likes it or not. This is the fate of fallen humanity.

Since God, who created heaven and earth, is one, all creations conceived by Him and the values established through creation must also become one. However, the result has been a division into two. This proves that we are in a fallen state. Therefore, the question becomes whether to follow the person of the heart or the person of the body, and what direction and method to take.

You must undoubtedly follow the direction of the person of the heart. To do this, what must you do? You must overcome the other. You must eliminate it. You cannot have both sides be good; you cannot have this and that. You must positively affirm one and negatively deny the other. You must clearly recognize that you possess both what you should affirm and what you should deny.

In speaking, there are words that are necessary for me and words that are unnecessary. In seeing, there are absolutely necessary things for achieving my inherent value, while there are opposing elements. The same applies to listening and thinking. When you wake up in the morning and gain a new awareness, you will have both an awareness that should be forgotten forever and an awareness that must not be forgotten. The results of that direction will determine the division of good and evil based on the direction related to you. This is why the teacher begins each day by making a good greeting before God.

Daily life determines one's destiny.
So how should I approach my daily life? I must start from good. When I become aware, I must prepare a greeting to start the day anew with God, and I must also set a plan for what I will do today. After starting the day with such a determination, I should reflect in the evening on whether I lived in accordance with that plan. When going to bed, I must be able to reflect on and settle the day.

Whether it is a month, a year, or ten years, among the quantities of good and evil, which side has been greater? In other words, between the quantities aimed at the purpose of the heart and those aimed at the purpose of the body, you must recognize where you stand.
The decision of whether I have left behind good or evil depends on which side was greater. If throughout my life I accumulate more good standards than evil ones, it will determine the fate of my return. Therefore, when you wake up in the morning and begin your daily life, you must inherit the whole and seek the points of discernment between good and evil. Since my individual existence has two purposes, it never compromises. Thus, it is impossible to avoid the fate of struggle, and there can be no peace. This is where the saying "life is suffering" comes from. Therefore, I must make a choice. I must resolve to absolutize the side I choose and push forward with it.

**The Path of Religion**

In following the direction of my heart, the opposing force is the body, so the struggle to align the direction of the body with the direction of the heart continues not only until you die but also into the spiritual world. The question is, how will you overcome this limit while alive? How will you surpass the limit of return? Religion pursues this from the standpoint that it becomes the side of the heart and sees the side of the body as an enemy. Therefore, religion is the path of obedience, not the path of compliance. The journey is not a straightforward one but a paradoxical one. It is not a positive path but a negative one. It seeks to incorporate a facet of negativity to expand the positive aspect. This is why Christianity teaches to be meek and humble, to serve sacrificially. We humans dislike being meek and humble. We want to do things our own way. We want to do as we please. Moreover, humans do not want to bow their heads to anyone. They want to rise higher. This is the essence of our fallen nature.

Humanity's ancestors fell because they sought to rise to a position like God’s without maintaining their own position, aiming for God's highest purpose and trying to jump up. To restore this, we must jump down. Here, a decisive factor of negativity is necessary. So when do we do this? It cannot be postponed to a year or ten years later. It must be done now, at this moment. If you miss this time, it can easily become habitual.

To determine such a negative position, you must invite God into your daily life, stand on God's side, consult your conscience, and act in accordance with it. In conclusion, you must allow everything that your heart likes and reject everything that your heart does not like. You must refuse everything that the body desires. The body, when well-fed, wants to eat even better food, and when well-dressed, wants to wear even better clothes. The more it receives, the more it wants to receive.

**Determining Good and Evil**

So where is good and evil determined? Good and evil are not determined elsewhere. You might say, "It’s because society is like that..." The issue of youth today, which is a global problem, arises from where? Is it because the environment is bad, or because the environment does not suit my heart?

Humans seek freedom and want to live freely. However, this freedom is not a freedom without any limits. Freedom that departs from the law cannot exist. If the eye claims to be free and jumps out, can it survive? The eye cannot exist apart from the laws it is bound to. If it departs from the law, it loses its value. You must understand this.

Good and evil are not in the grand society or the world. They are right within you. They exist within yourself. Today’s world consists of 3.6 billion such individuals. The problem lies here. So where does the origin of evil lie? It is not in the family, society, nation, or world. Where does the origin of evil lie? The origin of evil lies within myself. The teacher thoroughly believed this when he was of your age.

When you see that there are two people of good and evil in your heart, when these two meet, they become four, and the 3.6 billion humanity becomes 7.2 billion fighting against each other. Until now, the world has been in conflict between the body and the heart, leading to the emergence of two worlds: one centered on the body’s purpose and the other on the heart’s purpose. Therefore, when the end comes, the harvest will manifest as the whole, which is today’s idealism and materialism.

The coexistence here is a state of coexistence where the struggle to deny each other continues. There cannot be coexistence in a state free from struggle. There cannot be coexistence in a state where peace is maintained and everyone is happy. From this perspective, the struggle between idealism and materialism must be resolved fundamentally. To resolve this, where do you place good? First, you must firmly establish a principled standard and then handle the subsequent positions based on that standard.

Since humans are centered on the heart, we must handle materialism centered on idealism. What is the decisive factor that can handle this? First, we must teach which is right and which is wrong. We must clearly teach which is above and which is below, which should remain and which should be eliminated. Therefore, when it is clearly understood that this teaching is more precious than communism or democracy, it will surely be corrected. However, if this is not clearly conveyed, it will not be corrected.

Today, the world of good and evil has spread from the individual and gradually expanded to bear fruit in the world, ultimately unfolding from just one person. We live in such a social environment today. We are living within this fence. This is life.

The question is how large my range is here. Some may go this way, while others may go the opposite way. You are also walking the path woven by your ancestors. Going towards evil means following the body, while going towards good means following the heart. In this case, when an individual starts with a standard of 100, if the good centered on the heart exceeds 50 to 60, the world will be governed through that lineage. What has religion been doing until now? There is only one thing to conquer in this world: it is not to conquer the family, not to conquer the nation, nor to conquer the world. It is to conquer oneself. Thus, religion has come to conquer oneself. You must understand this. I am always at the boundary between good and evil.

**If the Heart is Straight, One Can Discern Good and Evil**

So how should you start from here? If each person aims for 100, the body and heart should not be 50-50. Such a person will remain in the intermediate spirit world. They will stay in a buffer zone. Do you understand? If the body is at 60, they will undoubtedly go to hell. What is hell? It is a shadowy place. What is heaven? It is a shining place. That’s how it should be understood. Such a person will definitely go to a shadowy place. The further down you go, the darker it becomes.

Therefore, you must always think of your existence as the womb of good and evil. The teacher also struggled with this content when he was of your age. So what was the slogan he raised? "Before seeking to govern the universe, complete self-governance." This is the first principle in faith. In this regard, when you can complete the self and gain the autonomy to control the self, that is when there will be no conflict between your body and heart.

If you continue to live in such a state for a year or several years, you will have spiritual experiences. It will happen automatically. If you continue such a life, you will become quite spiritually sensitive. You will learn to discern good and evil. Living this way will make your heart straight. When the heart is straight, what happens? When a wave comes at a 90-degree angle, it can reflect it directly at a 90-degree angle.

In other words, if the heart is straight, it reflects the incoming wave purely as it is. If the wave comes at a 45-degree angle, it will surely reflect at a 45-degree angle. If the wave comes at a 90-degree angle, it will reflect 100 percent at a 90-degree angle. However, if the heart is distorted, it cannot reflect the incoming wave at a 45-degree angle but will let it flow at a 30-degree angle. Therefore, when you live this way, spiritual feelings will automatically respond in your heart. You must understand this joy.

When you pray or devote yourself, you will feel a power emerging from somewhere. A force that transcends you comes to you. It feels like the waves sent from a broadcasting station are being received through an antenna and connecting with your heart. The purer your heart is, the more it reflects the incoming angle at the same angle.

As the heart reflects, the body must also reflect to prevent depletion. If the incoming wave is blocked by the body, it cannot be reflected. However, if we can allow the incoming wave to pass through as it is, our body will act similarly to vibrating, and spiritual experiences will come automatically. Do you want to have spiritual experiences? Do you want to, or not? "I want to." Do you want to? "Yes." If you suddenly experience it, side effects will occur. It must happen naturally.

In spring, flowers bloom naturally from trees, but for a tree to bloom, it must grow enough to be able to bloom. If it is just starting to sprout, can it bloom? If you pull the tree to make it grow faster, will it work? If it gets uprooted, that’s the end. Flowers must bloom naturally. Therefore, the path of faith should not be rushed. It is a path that creates a thousand-year history, so rushing is not allowed.

**The Problem of Overcoming Basic Needs**

So what is your current problem? It is to strengthen your conscience so that the strengthened conscience can govern the body, meaning that the heart can lead the body.

So where is the limit of our body? When the heart fights with the body, what is the first thing it wants to win over? There will be something. What is it? It is appetite. It is about eating. The problem is how to overcome appetite to live a religious life. Do you eat to live? "Yes." You must eat, but humans should not live just for food.

Even Jesus, during his 40 days of fasting prayer, was tempted by Satan, saying, "If you are the Son of God, command these stones to become bread." (Matt 4:3) Jesus’ response to that was remarkable. "Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word that proceeds from the mouth of God." (Matt 4:4) What does it mean to live by? It means to live by the word, by truth, that is, according to reason and law. Therefore, Jesus’ words to Satan were a rebuke asking why he lived by breaking God’s laws.

Thus, the most pressing issue is eating. Eating is the enemy. You must realize this. The primary enemy is eating. What is the next enemy? It is clothing. What comes next? It is living. The issues of food, clothing, and shelter are the problems. The body, if not careful, can easily fall into this. The body wants to eat good food without hesitation when it is available. It also wants to wear good clothes if they are available. That is how the principle is set. It has been created that way from the beginning.

However, because humanity has fallen, we cannot eat whatever we want. We must eat only two-thirds. One-third should not be taken. We should not take all three-thirds. Also, when dressing, we should not wear the best or the finest. Why? Because if we do, we will stand in a position of wearing the completed products of the satanic world.

**Eat, Dress, and Live Centered on the Heart**

The body always wants to live in the best place. On the other hand, what about the heart? When it comes to eating, it does not want to eat the best alone; it wants to share. The heart thinks this way. If there are two parties, the heart feels guilty if it eats a little more because it thinks that if I eat a little more, you will eat less. Even among siblings, a conscientious sibling does not boast about having eaten one more. If they boast about this, it can lead to trouble. Such things happen often among children. They all want to have the best. Educating such children is a significant issue.

People want to wear good clothes. However, a purely conscientious person feels ashamed when wearing good clothes. The heart does not think it is good. Why? Because it feels sorry for those who cannot wear good clothes. The heart teaches this. Isn’t that right?

Also, living in the best house in the world would be wonderful, right? However, the heart thinks otherwise. It believes that one should not live like that alone. The heart thinks it is okay to live in a good house after making everyone else happy first, but it should not be just for oneself. If one denies this, they will fall from being a person of the heart to being a person of the body.

If there is the richest person in South Korea, how can we know whether they will remain the richest for long or not? A person who earns money to brag about it will not last long. Money does not want to be with such a person. Do you understand? This is because all things are meant to be governed by humans, and since the center of a person is the heart, money prefers to be governed before the heart. Although money may come to that person, it will try to part ways with someone who prioritizes material things. Therefore, such a person’s end is miserable.

However, what if one earns money not for oneself but for the country or the world? What if I earn money and say I will use it not for myself but for the country? Would money like such a person or not? If one spends ten million won for oneself and not a penny for others, what would happen? On the other hand, if one spends not a penny for oneself but ten million won for others, what would happen? Would money be sad or happy? Happy? "Yes."

When it comes to eating, if I decide to eat bad food and give good food to others, does the heart dislike it or like it? The feeling of giving to others is better than the feeling of having eaten a good meal myself. You should try it. It is indeed true. When you give, how many people feel happy? The recipients feel happy.

We reflect on how much effort You have put in to establish the Unification Church on this Korean territory, and how much hardship Jesus Christ must have endured alongside that. We ask that this Unification Church be allowed to receive glory as a reward for You and fulfill Your wishes.

Please remember Your children gathered here at this time. While there are many believers and people celebrating the birth of Jesus Christ today, how many are there who, like us, recall that time and celebrate this moment while looking forward to the world of Christ tomorrow? In this sense, we realize that we are indeed in a precious and blessed position.

Many people celebrate this day, but if they do so without knowing its significance, we, as insignificant ones, celebrate this day with joy, knowing Your circumstances and feeling Your heart, thanks to Your labor and efforts. We sincerely thank You for this grace.

Father, at this time, bless the children of unity scattered throughout South Korea and bless Your children scattered around the world. As countless nations and Christians celebrate this day, may Your glorious hand be with them. We earnestly ask that Your infinite love and grace may forever be with them wherever they are serving sincerely.

Father, may all that we gather here to commemorate this day become a source of pride before Your will, and may the path Your son has walked until now become a foundation of hope. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

From this time forward, please protect all matters with Your love and grace. May all people be allowed to prepare for a glorious moment and dwell in Your grace. **Message** Today, as you all know, is Christmas, a holy day celebrated by Christians around the world. 

Celebrating the birth of Jesus in the most meaningful way
While many Christians celebrate the day Jesus was born, there are none who celebrate the life He lived on this earth. Furthermore, throughout the 2000 years since His passing, there are no celebrations reflecting on His whereabouts or the efforts made to develop Christianity. Therefore, we must celebrate not only the day Jesus was born but also His life, and at the same time, we must praise the achievements He left behind through the historical process after His coming and going.

So, what was the purpose of His birth, passing through His life and the historical era? It is solely to fulfill the will of the Father. He was born for this purpose, fought for it, and walked the path of pioneering without rest. Thus, it is essential that individuals capable of inheriting the Father's will emerge, and families formed by such individuals must arise, and tribes, nations, and the world formed from those families must also emerge. Without such a world, we cannot achieve the purpose of celebrating the birth of Jesus Christ.

Jesus was born because there was a will to be fulfilled. We must understand that fulfilling that will is the purpose of Jesus' meaningful life. Therefore, we must dedicate our entire lives to the will of Jesus, that is, the will of God, and become the necessary entities before that will as the embodiment of Jesus' holy desire. This is the most significant thing we can do to celebrate this day. We must find such individuals and families to celebrate this day, and we must find such tribes, nations, and worlds to celebrate this day to truly celebrate the day Jesus was born.

From this perspective, we, the members of the Unification Church, must find and dedicate to the Father the individuals, families, tribes, nations, and states that Jesus sought to find in His place. This is the meaningful work that allows us to celebrate this holy day.

You all know well how Jesus came to die. Because families could not uphold Him, tribes could not uphold Him, nations could not uphold Him, the foundation prepared for 4000 years within God's will was shattered, and because that foundation was broken, Jesus Christ, who came to establish that will, had no choice but to bear the cross. We must understand this tragic fact.

Knowing that the will was not fulfilled, we have the responsibility to fulfill that will. Therefore, we cannot help but think that this holy day holds even greater significance for us who celebrate it today.

Jesus intended to establish the nation of Israel, but due to failure, we must offer this land of Korea and the thirty million people as the Third Israel before the Father. Since now is the time to do this, if we succeed in this endeavor, we can conclude the meaningful will that Jesus has worked hard to fulfill from His birth through His life and up to now.

Thus, we must do our utmost to make this nation align with Jesus' will and dedicate it to Him. This is the responsibility we must fulfill before celebrating this day. To do so, we must resolve to make even greater efforts in pioneering our lives and environment. Only then can this day become a more valuable day of celebration.

We must understand how much Jesus longed for a nation that could be established before the will, how much He longed for a church that could be established before the will. We must also understand how much He longed for families like Joseph's and Zechariah's, and how much He longed for Joseph and Mary and their brothers. Considering these issues, we must recognize that there has been no group capable of fulfilling Jesus' longings from families to tribes, churches, and nations.

We must fulfill the individuals and families that Jesus so dearly desired. We must fulfill the tribes He longed for, the churches He longed for, and the nations He longed for. This is the responsibility we must bear as those who understand Jesus' circumstances and innermost feelings. We must do everything possible to bring about such results. We must deeply realize that unless we inherit and accomplish this work at the cost of all kinds of sacrifices, we cannot complete Jesus' will.

Unification Church members must fulfill Jesus' resentment
The years 1970 and 1971 are the most important periods in this end-time era, and this Christmas, December 25, 1970, may become the last day of celebration that divides the past era from the new era for us Unification Church members. Considering that 1970 and 1971 have distinctly different characteristics, we must pledge our hearts in loyalty as we send off this day and welcome the new year of 1971.

From the moment Jesus was born in the nation of Israel, He had to receive the love of God while also receiving the love of the Jewish nation nurtured in that love. Moreover, He had to receive the love of Judaism and the love of the entire Joseph family. However, Jesus Christ did not receive such love. He had to love the nation of Israel, the church, the tribes, and the Joseph family, even though He did not receive love from them. Despite being in such a position, He ultimately became a parent, a brother, a tribe, a church, and a nation that could not love. How tragic is this fact? You must understand this.

Jesus died on the cross because He could not fulfill this.
At some point, we must be able to love nations and peoples from the same standpoint as Jesus Christ. Without love, we cannot indemnify the sorrow of Jesus and God's sorrow. Because God's sorrow and Jesus' sorrow arose from the painful path of the cross, we Christians today cannot enter heaven without resolving this sorrow as we face the end times.

God's purpose in establishing the nation of Israel over a period of 4,000 years was to enable love for Jesus. Additionally, God's nurturing of Judaism for 4,000 years was also to allow people to love Jesus as the High Priest. The choice of Joseph's family among numerous tribes was to ensure that this nation would love Jesus more than anyone else. In this way, God wanted people to love Jesus through their nations, churches, and tribes.

Furthermore, after receiving the love of the Israelite nation that God prepared for Him, Jesus, as the Son who received God's love more than anyone, desired to love Joseph's family, Judaism, and the nation of Israel. It was Jesus' wish to love Judaism, the nation of Israel, and Joseph's family, which God had prepared for Him to love. However, because Jesus could not love these, they remained as His sorrow.

Thus, God's sorrow is that the nation, church, and tribe prepared to love Jesus did not love Him, and Jesus' sorrow is that He could not love Judaism, the Israelite nation, and Joseph's family, which were prepared to love Him. Because this sorrow of God and Jesus remains, we members of the Unification Church must resolve it today. To do this, we must have a nation like Israel from which we can love, a denomination like Judaism, and a tribe like that.

This is where the problem lies. Therefore, the nation of Israel that could not love Jesus, the Judaism that could not love Jesus, and the tribe of Joseph that could not love Jesus must establish a standard that can love Him. 

The issue is how to create an environment where we can love Jesus. From this perspective, if South Korea is the Third Israel today, we must ask whether South Korea itself stands in a position to love Jesus, whether the Christianity of South Korea stands in a position to love Jesus, and whether there are specific families like Joseph's family that can uphold the Lord's will and love Him.

The meaning of "family" in the Unification Church 

So, to what stage have we come? We have established the Unification Church. This is akin to restoring the lost Judaism. Today, the Unification tribes are similar to restoring the lost clans and reuniting lost brothers. In this sense, today, we in the Unification Church are one family. Without the connection of brotherhood, clans cannot be formed. Moreover, before connecting to the bond of brotherhood, neither the church nor the nation can emerge. A nation cannot be formed either.

Therefore, it is our mission in the Unification Church to connect based on this bond of brotherhood. In this sense, the term "family" is established. Through families, the bond of brotherhood is formed, and this term "family" can be the foundation for creating the kingdom of heaven. Therefore, members of the Unification Church must understand that they use the term "family."
Therefore, today, members of the Unification Church must share the love that Jesus could not give and receive. Older members should love younger members as Jesus' parents could not love Jesus.
