May the citizens of this capital city feel their own shortcomings before you and have a yearning for you, so that their hearts can unite with the hopes of countless ancestors in the heavenly world, as well as the hopes of millions of saints, and may the day come soon when they can praise your glory. Therefore, may all that happens centered around Seoul be something that you can rejoice in.

When I think that we, the Unification Church, still have a significant mission to fulfill, I hope that your love will be even more with us this morning as we close out 1970. I thank you for your protection over the past year. May you personally lead all our actions and endeavors in the future, and may your infinite heart of compassion abundantly dwell in the paths we fight and pioneer, Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

Today is the last holy Sabbath of 1970, a year that will not come again, so please remember us. Father, if you require us to make new resolutions, please come secretly to each of our hearts and instruct us. You have gathered us to fulfill a new historical mission, so may we welcome the year 1971 with renewed determination, self-awareness, and pledges.

This morning, in the capital city of Seoul, countless of your children from many denominations are looking towards your will, yet they do not know the path they should take at the end. How desperately are they struggling? Please clarify their path, and through the rumors that come or the results that appear, may you work so that they can be embraced in your arms, Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this. May you personally be with the remaining days, and may you also be with the countless children who are dedicating their hearts here, and remember your daughters who are fighting alone.

As they come to understand all the circumstances that made it necessary for you to send them out like this, may their desires align with your desires, Father, and may their lives as pioneers be in accordance with your pioneering position. Entrust to them your work for the nation and the world, so that they may become your beloved daughters who lead in loving this nation and the world.

Moreover, since this is a 40-day pioneering period, please encourage your children who are walking the path of your will during this time. Your will cannot be stopped, and it cannot be hesitated, so we must unify with all our strength and push forward with the heavenly position. May this morning be a time when we can once again reaffirm this commitment, Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

I sincerely thank you for watching over us throughout this year and leading us by observing our surroundings. I also truly appreciate that you have allowed us to achieve great results this year and to reveal the current position of the Unification Church in a straightforward manner. Now, not only in society but also in each household, may you help the young children realize that they are part of the Unification group that can be the vanguard of a new era, and may they be blessed to participate in the same rank before your will, becoming eternal descendants of the everlasting Father.

Furthermore, please bless your beloved children who are blessed. May you once again give new instructions to the families scattered around the world, so that they may unite and form the one nation they desire, and dedicate that nation to you with all their sincerity and loyalty. Realizing that there is a mission that must be devoted to this Korean land, may your children, who know how to praise tomorrow's victory and long for their homeland, become such children, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

May all their lives, in which they yearn for your will and fight for it, not stray from your love, and may everything within that remain united and prepared to be completely offered before you, becoming a group of unity, a lineage of unity, and a global citizen of unity, I earnestly request and wish for this.

Father, your inadequate children are bowed down here, so please help them discover for whom they exist. When we think about what we have moved for and what we have felt until now, may we grieve for having invested everything for the fleeting self, for the lonely self that found no results, and may we become holy beings who can completely dedicate ourselves before you for the eternal heavenly legacy. I earnestly hope and wish that this time may be one where we can once again make a deep resolution before you.

Please remember each of us, and may you protect and nurture us so that we can fulfill the mission and responsibility entrusted to us in the remaining era. I thank you for everything that has happened this year. Please protect us in the remaining days, Father.

As countless people gather their hearts in one place to set plans for the new year, may every such gathering be united around your will and move forward. I ask once again in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Sermon> When we look at today, we see that the past is connected and the future is connected. In other words, the present cannot exist by itself. 

In this regard, when we consider our individual selves, we are the embodiment of the past and the starting point of the future. And the present self that we are is not an isolated individual, but a self that demands a central position in connecting Korea and the world, where all are related. Therefore, we say that we need the past centered on ourselves, we say that we need the present centered on ourselves, and we say that we need the future centered on ourselves.

The current position of God and humanity
No one thinks outside of themselves. They think of the past centered on themselves, they think of the present centered on themselves, and they think of the future centered on themselves. And when thinking, they do not want to focus on bad things. They want to think of good things centered on the past, present, and future.

Therefore, a person must have a good past, must carve out a position that can be good in the present, and must move forward envisioning a future that is worthwhile and valuable based on that established foundation. For that result to manifest, it must not only be good for their own life but also for the nation and the world. This is the position we humans find ourselves in today.

In this position, when we think, is it not the same for God as it is for us humans? If we look at it centered on God, we can think of the process through which God began creation and established the created beings, and the past when He created humanity as the center of the purpose of creation. And we can think of the miserable history of restoration that has continued from the time that brought about the unwanted result of the fall until now.

In other words, when we look at God's past, what is it that cannot be forgotten in that reflection? At first, of course, He must have rejoiced infinitely at the results of the creation's achievements, but with infinite hope and expectation, there must have been a time of joy when He looked upon humanity as the center that could showcase the realization of tomorrow's creation. However, due to the unexpected results of this tremendous fall, He had to embark on a path of painful struggle over the ages, and He must now take on the mission of a pioneer once again—not with hope, but with sorrow in every heart and in every encounter, hoping to overcome the sorrowful peaks. The more we reflect on that past, the more it becomes a history that amplifies sorrow.

Then, when we look at God's current position as He pioneers for the restoration of heaven, what is the difference between the past and the present? Today, there are many religious people and many Christians in this vast world. However, when we consider how many religious organizations or children who believe in such religions can truly restore the desires of God lost in the Garden of Eden before the God who has come forth with sorrow until now, we realize that the present is indeed overwhelming. The God who is in this present is not a joyful God, but rather a sorrowful God, a God who cannot have hope, a God who can only regret in despair.

The crucial point of transforming sorrow into joy
So, if we observe the world from God's perspective in light of this reality, where is the point of new hope, the foundation of new hope on this earth? 

There are many countries on this planet. Among them, there are countries that boast of their civilization as advanced nations, and there are countries and nations that pride themselves on being blessed in the world and blessed as a people. However, if we look beyond their self-perception, we see that God's expectations and hopes are not there.

Then, if we consider that this insignificant Unification Church, which has walked the path of persecution on Korean soil, is the center of the hope that God currently has for the world, it can be seen as an incredibly significant and astonishing grace, while at the same time, it can also be a fearful thing.

If the Unification Church stands in such a position today, its current position is one that is facing a precious and monumental global event. When we reflect on the histories up to now, they have been histories of sorrow, but the present centered around the Unification Church today must not be connected to a history of sorrow. This moment must be the most crucial point in history where we must transform sorrow into joy and affirm the results of joy.

Then, when we compare the countless ancestors who have followed the path of the will or the providential will throughout the historical ages with us, the members of the Unification Church who are facing this will today, we find that all the devotion and loyalty of the ancestors in the past ultimately left a history that could not be expected before God's wishes and instead increased sorrow. Therefore, if the mission to represent the joy and hope of heaven today lies with the Unification Church, the mission entrusted to each individual member of the Unification Church is immense. Thus, we must not cause God to be disheartened again, and we must present the thoughts of joy and hope before Him. We must realize that we have this historical mission.

Many prophets and sages have come and gone in the past, but if they reflect on their past, they would not rejoice. That is a past that must be cast aside. Even if a nation has a cultural sphere that can boast of its excellence in the historical era, that good past cannot be a source of pride. It is merely events that will vanish in God's sorrow.

Therefore, our Unification Church must be able to leave all the efforts and achievements of the past, where countless prophets and sages poured out their loyalty and devotion while walking the path of death, as joy in God's deep heart and as conditions for reflection. If this responsibility lies with us, the responsibility of being a member of the Unification Church today is indeed immense.
When viewed this way, we cannot help but think that God sees the daily lives we lead and the years we live, or the 10 or 20 years we will live in the future, as more important than the events left behind by countless prophets and sages who came and went in the past, which have become mere memories. Therefore, we must not recreate the history of sorrow or live a life of repetition; rather, we must fulfill our responsibility to absolve the history of sorrow and create a new history. This is the mission of us, the members of the Unification Church.

Thus, if the present does not become a moment that accompanies God's sorrow from the past, nor a present that can be praised at some point in the future, then a joyful history cannot remain for the future, nor can it be a condition for reflecting on and longing for the present when looking back from the future. Today's present must inevitably become a time and period that flows along with history. If that happens, we will come to realize that the position we find ourselves in today is incredibly significant, as it will remain as a sorrowful history that will be condemned in the future.

What we must leave behind at this present point
When considering the existence of a person, there is no difference between the person of today and those who came and went in the past. The desire to become the center of global values is the same for both ancient and modern people. From some perspectives, while the present may be in a worse position than the past in longing for goodness and fighting for it, we must absolutely not forget that the standards imposed upon us by the demands of our era and history are tremendous.

If the steps we take in our Unification Church become the foundation of history, the spirit of history, and the path that can absolve all past sorrows, then the lives of those of you walking that path will not be meaningless but will be lives that move forward. This is not a linear progression but a flat, and further, a three-dimensional progression. All the prophets and sages of historical eras would wish for you to become such individuals. Furthermore, God will hope that we become central beings who are not lacking in being presented as the center of such history.

When considering this issue, you must always be aware that each individual is not merely a solitary existence but a being standing amidst historical centers, historical desires, and historical expectations.

Now, as we will go through many historical processes in the 1970s, 1980s, or even the 2000s and beyond, what is it that we must leave behind at this present moment? In the 1970s, there will be temporal limitations as the Unification Church emerges. There will also be peaks that must be surpassed at this present point. From the perspective of purpose, there will be personal peaks, familial peaks, and peaks at the national, ethnic, and global levels. However, the moment in which we can surpass those peaks is not something that occurs twice in the era of the world or in the providential history of God; it exists only once. The question is when and by whom that once-in-a-lifetime moment will be passed. While we are in the process of meeting such a time, it is difficult to assert and confidently surpass it by saying, "This is definitely the time."

From this perspective, when the moment of the peak curves within our current living sphere, and when my life and heart transcend the world, if there is someone who earnestly thinks, "I cannot miss this once-in-a-lifetime moment," that person will be extremely wise. Such a person will represent the heart of the greatest sages and the lives of the most righteous. If such a person pursues an ideal, they will be able to stand at the pinnacle of that pursuit.

Therefore, the present moment is not an ordinary one. Especially during this period of the 1970s, which the Unification Church is traversing, it is not merely a wave within an ordinary era, nor is it just a single indicator or principle. It is a period that can achieve the pinnacle of historical eras. Thus, we must recognize how precious and significant the present we are living in today is.

Therefore, we must fulfill our duty of loyalty at this time and be able to pledge the results of victory. We must also invest our desires, our heightened loyalty, and our sincere intentions to leave behind a present moment that is full and complete, without any gaps in every direction. This will be the wish of our ancestors from the past, the standard that people in the world today strive for in their hearts, and the highest expectation that our descendants in the future will have for their ancestors.

This is true not only when considering human history but also when considering the history of restoration. God, looking at the present, will want to make it a foundation from which to settle the regrettable past and proudly push forward into the future. However, if there is no moment, no single instant to decisively determine and surpass, then the sorrowful history cannot be settled, and a joyful present will not remain in the future.

When considering the issue of having no choice but to inherit a sorrowful history, we must not escape from here, even if we face any trials and tribulations. We must not hesitate but rather strike decisively for a peak that God desires and that the past, present, and future all yearn for. Thus, if we become determined individuals and a determined Unification altar capable of pledging the overall decisive victory, this will lead to a victorious foundation that can comprehensively settle the history of the world. The question is whether we ourselves, our church, can become that foundation.

The Unification group must bear the joy of the nation's unfaithfulness
When considering the Unification Church today, it has a history of over 20 years. When we look at what we can boast about during those 20 years, or what we can boast about in God's providential history, we find that there is only the history of the nation's unfaithfulness, that is, the past of the nation's disbelief.

Having gone through three administrations of the Republic of Korea, we have faced condemnation from numerous denominations and the nation itself, and we have been cornered in our living environment. We must recognize that this does not provide any conditions to boast about before God.

Reflecting on the past history, we must understand that it was a sorrowful period that inherited the betrayal of disbelief in God's heart, who has continued a history of sorrow. Furthermore, that history has stimulated the shame of this nation, provoked its incompleteness, and stirred up individual disbelief, prompting each person to once again seek hope.

Therefore, it is of utmost importance for us to transform the sorrowful history of the Unification Church into a joyful history at some point. This is what God desires, what the Republic of Korea, which has betrayed and opposed us until now, desires, and what the countless ancestors who have come and gone in Korea desire. When the providential anchor is dropped to decisively position Korea in the heavenly fortune, and when the countless spirits in the spiritual world who have come forth to fulfill God's will realize that the created world on earth must inevitably leave behind the results of sorrow, who can leave behind a joyful result? Not God, not other nations, not other people. It must be the Unification group of our church, which appears insufficient, weary, and immature in today's view. When we think of this tremendous reality, you should feel the heartbeat and pulse of your heart as something different from the usual. To achieve this, you must invest sincerity into your lives.

If you have lived without knowing that the teacher has surpassed his ultimate limit, that ignorance will remain as sorrow. Therefore, from now on, you must follow the standards that can be known. It is impossible to participate in the ideal world without matching the pace to connect with the peak and without possessing the value of having surpassed that peak.

God who wants to embrace a greater standard
So, what will the teacher, who is leading the Unification Church today, choose? When that time comes, will he think he can surpass it alone? Or will he think he can surpass it together with the followers, the blessed families? The teacher wants to surpass not only the Unification Church but also the nation, the state, and further, Asia and the world, centered on the Unification Church. He wants to surpass it in the environment of spring, in the position where he can determine the center.

From this, we can see that God does not want to limit that scope to individuals but wishes to expand it to families, tribes, nations, the entire world, and even the cosmos, wanting to surpass that moment together. When we think of God's heart in this way, we realize that He has undoubtedly not had a joyful day until now. This is because such a day occurs only once, and God's heart and the heart of the leader desire to welcome that historical moment together with all humanity.

God has not yet had a time to praise individual victories on a global scale. He has not had a time to praise families globally, nor has He had a time to achieve global victory through any particular tribe, nor has He had a victorious position centered on nations.

When an individual does something good, God's heart desires to connect that to the world. If a family is doing well, He does not want to praise only that family; He wants to connect the goodness of that family to the goodness of the world. If a tribe does something well, He wants to connect that to the world, and if a nation does something well, He hopes that it will not remain only with that specific nation but will be recognized as a particular international entity and remain as a global citizen. Therefore, we must understand that God has not been able to praise individuals, families, tribes, or nations with a joyful heart until now.

We must become a Unification Church that can stand closer to God's heart
Considering God's position and reflecting on the past and present of the Unification Church, we must recognize that there has never been a time when we could boast about ourselves globally as Unification Church members. There has never been a time when we could boast as families or as tribes. Furthermore, even if the entire Republic of Korea welcomes us, we must question whether we can stand in a position to boast before the world. We know that simply being welcomed by Korea does not allow us to joyfully boast to the world. In this light, we must seek to establish the Republic of Korea in such a position before it can be globalized and can boast to the world.

When we consider the destiny of the Unification Church, it may seem like a sorrowful destiny, but when we think about how God has endured and persevered until now, it may be the path that can bring us closest to God's internal heart.

If there is a time to boast about individuals, we should not only seek to match that with individual times but should welcome it as a time to boast together with families, and not only with families but also with tribes, nations, and the world. This is what God's heart desires. In other words, it is God's deep and great heart to welcome a time when we can simultaneously boast about individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world.

When we think about this, we must consider how the Unification Church can remain until such a time and how many people within the Unification Church can think about such a future. Even if we dedicate our lives to the path of suffering, if we think of it with sorrow, we cannot connect that to a time that can be left as a time for the world. In light of these facts, we must recognize that the Unification group, which has emerged with determination and resolution today, is in a position where we must reaffirm our commitment with innovative content.

What we have been working towards until now is not to seek the price of today's sacrifice but to praise a central value that can manifest the connections of all people and all ages centered on thousands of years of history. This is the direction and path that Unification thought aims for. This is because God has brought it forth in this way. God desires to praise the liberation of individuals while simultaneously hoping for a liberation that can praise all families, all nations, and all countries.

A person who can leave today's joy as tomorrow's joy
When considering this issue, we must ask whether there has been a cultural and civilizational framework with appropriate traditional thought or spiritual support. Until now, there has been no such cultural and civilizational framework. We must recognize that civilizations lacking such traditional thought or spiritual support have flowed away through the historical eras.

However, if a new civilizational framework is established based on the ideological support derived from Unification thought, which seeks the common good and the common justice, and if we can connect today's joy to the value of the whole, pledging our lives alongside the world, and praising the value of connections with the world, then that civilization will undoubtedly be eternal. If that happens, that civilization will become a framework that can inherit and pass down a culture more new and three-dimensional than any nation that has been able to shine and boast of its history throughout the historical process.

Today, you all think you must live well and succeed. However, the desire to live well and succeed within the confines of a family centered on a surname, such as Kim, is vastly different from the desire to succeed and live well within the global context. The former represents a life closer to the past, while the latter represents a life closer to the future.

A person who seeks only today's joy centered on themselves within the limits of today will inevitably clash with tomorrow. Today's joy is inherited by tomorrow. Therefore, we must not merely pass today’s joy as today’s joy but must carry it forward so that it can be left for the future. When that happens, it will possess infinite value.
Such a thought, one that does not center on oneself but rather pursues the summit of victory centered on the world, hopes that heaven and earth, the spirits who have come and gone in the past, humanity in the present, and future descendants can all raise their hands in praise, declaring this place to be a global summit where all people can rejoice in the arrival of spring. If we hope for such a place, then no matter how great the suffering of today’s life may be, that suffering can be seen as a pain that can overcome and conquer the summit. A life that can remain as a material to determine the summit cannot be conquered by anyone.

So when we ask which is more precious, it is not the self-centeredness that is valuable, but the world-centeredness that we can think of as precious. Why is that? Because God has not been able to boast of such a time throughout any historical era until now.

Then what time does God wish to boast about? Perhaps it is the joy when the Magi came to offer gifts and worship at the birth of Jesus, or the joy of the angels rejoicing, which could be the joy of birth, but it does not become the joy of inheriting great achievements. In other words, it was not the praise and worship that filled God with joy by completing the great work of creation and receiving the response and agreement of all creation, but rather the praise and worship that began with a view toward the future.

That joy was the joy of starting out while going through the process and affirming the joy of the future, not the joy of achieving the global summit of future purposes. Although they started with joy at the arrival of the long-awaited Jesus, we know that the miserable fate of Christianity remained because they lacked the purpose of that beginning. We also know that the event that compounded the sorrow of human history was none other than the crucifixion of Jesus. Because of this event, God faced a sorrowful turn greater than that at the fall of Adam and Eve, which we understand was manifested in three hours of darkness.

However, the Almighty God had to fulfill the desire to leave a global summit, so He determined that at some time and in some place, He must establish one person as the center and has nurtured Christianity through thousands of years of suffering history until now. This Christianity, found as a result of suffering, is meant to restore and indemnify the history of suffering, yet today, among believers in Christianity, where is there anyone who can adorn the history of suffering, and where is there anyone who possesses the value that can be found as a result of that suffering?

While sitting in a position of heavenly providence, when we think about such issues, we cannot help but feel despair. However, rather than merely lamenting in despair, we must feel a sense of heavenly mission from that despair and raise a new movement to strive harder. The origin of such a movement cannot be sought in any place on this earth; the fulfillment of God’s will and the fulfillment of humanity’s desires are impossible without it. If there are those who struggle for such a time, suffer for such a time, and hope and worry for the emergence of such a time, then from there, a new history and a new world can begin. Otherwise, we must recognize that we cannot even think about it. Thus, today, our Unification Church cannot help but follow that path.

As Jesus died on the cross, He said, “I will come again. The bridegroom will surely come, so prepare yourselves as brides.” He promised a day of the wedding feast that could remain as a boast before all people and all ages. Then, is that wedding feast Korean? It is not Korean; it is global. It is not ethnic; it is trans-ethnic. It is not sectarian; it is trans-sectarian. It does not only take place on earth; it is something that God participates in, and the center is God. The God who is the center wishes to welcome that day not in sorrow but in joy and jubilation.

This is the time of the global summit, the time when all people meet the peak of hope, and the time to conclude the sorrowful history. Moreover, this is the time when the center of the whole can be determined, all sorrowful histories can be removed, and a new history of joy can begin.

When we consider such issues, we must ask whether the Unification Church has ever had such a day in the ideal path it desires today. The path we have walked until now has been a path of tears. At times, we have come forth while avoiding the eyes of many crowds, in the shadows or in narrow paths, affirming this path. However, when we think that this was not what God was satisfied with or desired, we must awaken today. We must awaken more than the nation of Israel, more than the Jewish sects, and more than the apostles who followed Jesus.

We must recognize that this tremendous heavenly providence is bound to the place where we are sitting today. Each of our actions must be able to emerge as the flower of history, and each of our thoughts must be able to spread as the fragrance of history. We must become the cleaners who can remove all the laments of humanity. Furthermore, we must realize that we are historical representatives who must offer indemnity to God, who has wrinkles in His heart of love and whose heart is pierced with nails that no one can pull out. In this regard, it is not a problem if our outward appearance is shabby. If my outward appearance is shabby, I must think of the saints who walked in an inwardly shabby manner throughout the historical ages and be able to pledge before heaven that I will offer indemnity and restore them from the position of a historical representative.

Therefore, if one finds themselves in a position of self-satisfaction, that satisfaction can be a satisfaction that can be shared with all of humanity, not just personal satisfaction. This is the path that has been traced out as the providence of restoration and the history of humanity. For this, countless sacrifices have been made, and a history of blood has been left behind. Therefore, you must understand that the purpose of that nation is not just to make me happy.

To carry out the re-creation history that God desires, do the members of the Unification Church today truly know that God is present? Do they truly feel the presence of God in their lives and know that He is working in contact with their cells? God is not only the God of the past; He is also the God of the present and the future.

If God was sorrowful in the past and is sorrowful in the present, then He must become the God of the future who can only be joyful if someone blocks that sorrow. Who will block God’s sorrow and transform it so that He can rejoice? Which individuals, families, tribes, nations must do so?

That nation must not be a nation swept away by the currents of the world but must be a nation that stands at the forefront, fighting within that current to lead the world’s trends. Only then can it become a nation that can represent the world. When we think about such issues, this cannot be anything but the most serious problem.

If there is someone who has that awareness, then this nation at this time does not simply refer to me. It is I who stands in place of the resurrection of history, I who stands at the very summit of the age. To speak in terms of a tree, I am the fruit that can be borne at the end of the branch. In other words, I am not the one who laments and sighs in sorrow; rather, no matter what difficulties and hardships I face, I can digest them into joy, and this nation is one that can guarantee that life for God in the past, present, and future. But have you become such a nation?

When we think of God, who could not retreat from the path of sorrow in the past, even if I face an unjust situation where sorrow is compounded, retreat is not something I can even dream of.

If God had thought of retreat, what would have happened to humanity today? The One who has maintained that position is our Father, my Father, and because we are the sons who have received the flesh and blood of that Father, we have the responsibility to repay and settle the debt of that Father. Therefore, we must have the heart to endure efforts and sacrifices that are several times greater than what God has done. When we go forth with the determination to comfort God, a heart of desire arises in you that can bring joy to God.

When we are pushed into a sorrowful position like that of God, if we say, “I want to die,” joy will not come forth. Even when placed in a position where God has labored, where the path of death intersects, if we can say, “Do not worry. I will leave my blood on that foundation to ensure that your path of suffering will be a meaningful point of hope for tomorrow,” we will become sons and daughters who leave behind a foundation of heart that history cannot surpass and that history cannot crush. From there, God will carry out the re-creation history that He has desired.

From the determination that I will surely fulfill God’s wishes, the motivation for God’s new touch will arise. That is why Jesus, on the path of the cross, said, “Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will.” He also said, “Father, forgive them for their sins,” and even on the path of death, He loved His enemies. Knowing that loving those whom we cannot love is the heart of the Father, God manifested the Second Israel through the heart of Jesus who walked that path.

When we consider these facts, we must become people who are willing to dedicate our lives to God with a faith posture that can do the same. Without becoming such people, we must recognize that we cannot leave behind a good ancestry that can be cherished before the descendants of this age and the future.

How should we accept our environment? If happiness comes in the future for the Unification Church, we must not claim that happiness solely for the Unification Church. If there is something that the Unification Church can boast about, it must be something that can be boasted about together with all people. Even in the victory of the Unification Church, we must not think of it as a victory solely for the Unification Church.

If we have such a mindset, it will flow away. Such a person may receive the scorn of history, but they cannot be in a position to inherit the hopes of a new future. Such a foundation will not remain. When we think about this, we will realize that our own victory, our own glory, and our own joy are not in accordance with God’s will.

Among the blessed people, there may be those who lament their unhappiness because their partner does not match their heart. However, if there is such a person, they cannot be someone who understands the sorrow of God, who came forth for the future of heaven. If my partner is in such a position among many families, God will see this and understand the difference between my standard and that of my partner. Even if that partner is not satisfied, if I have a heart of gratitude before God, that becomes an absolute condition for God to grant blessings in the not-too-distant future. Therefore, we must become such people.

When a path of suffering arises that is difficult to overcome in one’s life, rather than lamenting that it is painful and unfair to sacrifice one’s life here, one should be able to embrace it as a glorious opportunity to walk together with heaven, an opportunity that will not come again. And the person who can say, “Father, please accept my life,” will not end there; rather, a new history will begin from there. Death, suffering, and lamentation will be settled with history, and hope will be reborn from there.

<Word> Today is the second day after Christmas and one of the days at the end of the year. From the perspective of the mission of the Unification Church, we are at the point of crossing over from the year 1970 to the new year 1971.

The correct attitude of a believer centered on the will
What we need to understand is that even though we say we are living centered on the will, we must always hold onto the relationship between ‘the will and me’ and ‘me and the will.’ This is the attitude of life for us believers. In other words, the will should not exist separately from me, nor should I exist separately from the will. God desires individuals aligned with the will, families aligned with the will, churches aligned with the will, and furthermore, nations and a world aligned with the will. Therefore, we must connect and unify from the individual to the world with the will.

From this perspective, when we look at the Unification Church, it was established for the will and is moving forward for the will. If the Unification Church was established for the will and is moving forward for the will, then it is certain that the people belonging to the Unification Church were born for the will and are moving forward for the will. The path the church takes and the position it finds itself in cannot exist outside of the will, nor can it go that way. Therefore, the people within the church must also exist because of the will, and they must live because of the will.

Otherwise, even if there are people who have lived for dozens of years, no matter how brilliant their past lives were or how they can boast of their past lives, or even if they are patriots who are revered before their nation, we must consider that their will may align with what the nation desires, but it does not align with the will of God who looks upon this nation. A person in such a position may be in a rewarding position for the country, but when viewed from the perspective of the will that God desires, that position does not align with God's will.

Therefore, no matter how much one is supported by the state or revered by many nations, it goes without saying that one must not deviate from that position and must align with God's will. Here, regardless of age or gender, and regardless of class, unless we establish a form of unity that can align with the will, individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world that the will demands cannot emerge.

The Bible says, "Do not worry about what you will eat or drink or wear. For the pagans run after all these things, and your heavenly Father knows that you need them. But seek first his kingdom and his righteousness, and all these things will be given to you as well." (Matthew 6:31-33) The kingdom referred to here is not a kingdom that conflicts with the will. It is a kingdom that can start with the will, go through the process with the will, and bear fruit with the will.

Therefore, everything that exists must arise with the will, must exist with the will, and must come to an end with the will. It goes without saying that without standing in this position, one cannot become an individual of the heavenly kingdom, nor can one become an individual, family, or society of that kingdom.

What kind of kingdom do you desire? That kingdom is not the same as the one you are living in today. Such a kingdom must eventually say goodbye. If you have a connection with such a kingdom, it is a connection with sin. You are well aware that you were born as a fallen descendant of humanity who could not establish a connection with the will and God's will from the beginning.

If they get caught, no matter how much they plead with the leader, it will be of no use. The leader cannot do anything either.

In order for us to advance to the point of hope, we must stand in a position to become children of God. As children before God, we must maintain the original value of creation that God had in mind, regardless of the historical path we go through. We must realize that there is infinite internal suffering of God in thinking about how He must maintain humanity in this way.

Women must fight for the nation. Now we have risen to that position, so we are sending women to the front lines centered around families. Now is the era of restoration and return centered on women. Do you understand? After that, there remains the era of national restoration and return that women must undertake, centered around the 38th parallel. That is why in the future, we must create female soldiers in South Korea to fight against the People's Army.

Today's men in Korea are pathetic. They are terrified of the communist party in the North, which is only one-third of their size. Women must fight against the communists to expel the satanic world that has been lured by women. Women must take down the communists. That is the fight we must engage in. Do you understand?

That is why in the future, established churches will follow the Unification Church. When the families of established church members come into the Unification Church, we will rest and then send them back to the land of South Korea. Thus, the entire South must become a land unified by Unification Thought, a land where God can love. When that happens, we will gather the women of blessed families in the barracks. We will mobilize all those aged 30 and under 33. Do you understand?

Blessed families must do this until they are 40 years old. Jesus could not exceed 40 years. Therefore, everyone must be mobilized until the age of 40 to fight against the communists on the front lines. If we do not do this, when will women participate in liberating the nation? Until now, the world has been entirely arranged by men. However, now women must do this work to establish a time of global unity. We must enter the original world centered around the nation that has been found.

In the future, the blessed families of the Unification Church will stand at the forefront as sentinels of the 38th parallel. This is inevitable. When women stand in such positions, you must supply ammunition from the rear. Would you want your wife to die? You must provide food and carry ammunition all night long. If that is not enough, you must say you will fight in place of your wife. When we engage in this mutual fight, you must report to the leader. Only then can we mobilize all at once to defeat the communists.

Women must fight for the nation. What are you fighting for now? You are fighting for your families, right? If you receive the blessing of the Unification Church, you must fight not for your families but for the nation of Abel. You must fight for the Republic of Korea. Thus, there must be the era of the revival of women, the era of the growth of women, and the era of the completion of women, going through these three stages. This is to complete individual restoration and the completion of the concept of the partner to propagate goodness. The propagation of goodness cannot be without the standard of the nation. We must understand that if a nation cannot propagate children of goodness and pass through the satanic world, there remains a historical mission to restore three generations of women.

Do you know why the communists are creating female soldiers? This shows in advance that women must fight against the communist forces. Now, then, Unification Church women, those who are willing to join the female soldiers, raise your hands. Will you do it or not? If not, you will perish. Do you want to perish or prosper? Those who want to perish, raise your hands. Everyone wants to prosper, right? Where? Under the skirt? That will not do. In the future, women must do this work. Women must inevitably walk this path. 

All men are like archangels. Therefore, I must make women fight once. So, men must invest. It cannot be helped if you feel bad. Among you, who likes to see their wives go out to evangelize? What are you looking at? (Laughter) After all that has been said, should you not go your own way? This is not a laughing matter. Such a time will surely come.

A three-year evangelization period that must mobilize everyone without exception. When the leader mobilizes families, some may say, "Could the leader really do that? He let us be during the 40-day evangelization period, so he will probably do the same this time." During the 40-day evangelization period, it passed by without much happening, but this three-year period cannot be skipped. There is no way out. If everyone else goes out and you stay behind to do business, you might as well be dead. Also, those who go out later must fulfill the entire period of time. Otherwise, it will be impossible. This is a path that must be taken anyway. Those who do not go have nothing to do with the leader.

So, why am I sending you out in reverse? It is because it is our destiny to fulfill the will. To fulfill the will, we must become ancestors of goodness and families of goodness, having relationships that we can boast about for eternity. In following the path of salvation, we must go for that nation and that righteousness, not for our personal desires and private happiness. It is not like what the communists say, "What is yours is mine, and what is mine is mine." The Unification Church's way is, "What is mine is yours, and what is yours is the Father's." It is completely different. What is mine is yours, and what is yours is whose? The conclusion is that it belongs to the Father. The communist way is that what is yours is mine, and what is mine is mine, but the Unification Church way is that the Father takes my place. The communist way is that one enters for oneself.

The communists tie everything to their personal interests, but from God's perspective, this cannot lead to development. So, is the Unification Church the church of Reverend Moon? "No." The Unification Church is the Unification Church of the Republic of Korea. The Unification Church does precious work, and it serves God while comparing how great that preciousness is with other things. This is what living the faith of the Unification Church is about.

If it is public, it will prosper. You cannot enter a place you like alone. You must find Cain and take him with you. Who is ruling the current world? The archangel, Satan, is ruling. Cain is in the archangel position, right? So, who must return this world to God? Cain must repent joyfully and return it. Since what stands in the position of Abel must be restored through Cain, those who seek to die will live, and those who seek to live will die.

Getting married is not for oneself. Did the teacher have a private marriage or a public one? "He had a public wedding." The teacher married a girl of 18 when he was 40; do you think he did so because he was infatuated with her? When the teacher turned 40, women around 30 who had graduated from university were lining up to marry him, and many women were waiting day and night for him to accept them. However, he disregarded all of them and took a girl who knew nothing and re-educated her.

When the teacher speaks in the Unification Church, there are people murmuring in the back. The teacher does not lie. He teaches because he has tried everything and knows it to be true, yet some people say he is lying with their eyes rolled back.

Do you believe in the Unification Church publicly or privately?

To establish righteousness in that kingdom, do not think about what to eat, what to wear, or what to drink. You have gathered here to leave behind a substance that can adapt to that kingdom. Even now, just meeting five people makes a day go by. Unification Church members do not realize how time passes when they are with the teacher. They come in the morning and stay until lunch and dinner, just sitting there. So what fun is that for the teacher? There are countless things to do in a day. Yet if he tries to send them away, they feel bad and sulk. When the teacher goes out, they expect him to come back soon, and they insist on staying until after midnight to see him.  
You may be able to do that, but the time for the teacher to have personal moments has all passed. Everything has changed. Just as the teacher is advancing, you must also devote yourselves to advancing in this personal restoration era.  
However, if you say you will do it alone, it will not work no matter how hard you try. If the teacher does the work of the personal era, you must cooperate and put in your efforts here, and God will recognize it with the same value. Likewise, when the teacher does the work of the family era, tribal era, national era, and global era, you must also be faithful according to that era and keep pace. God is making all preparations for you to participate in this era, and he is mobilizing you to join in. You should not be unaware of this and sulk or frown. You must understand this.  
Do not miss the time to inherit God's kingdom.  
There will come a moment when you can inherit God's kingdom through a single moment. You must be ready for that moment. Therefore, whether you like it or not, you must consider it an honor to follow what the teacher asks you to do. The will is being fulfilled whether you like it or not, even without your knowledge. That is why the teacher is officially establishing laws and organizing things. However, you do not understand this well.  
If you are in a position to carry God while being unaware of this, do you think you can sleep well at night? While I am sleeping, while I am walking, while I am playing or resting, I do not know how God's will will unfold. How can I claim to be a loyal subject and citizen of that kingdom if I do not know whether misfortune or happiness will dwell in that kingdom? Therefore, you must give all your sincerity, heart, will, and character to inherit the time of God's will.

You must live for His kingdom and His righteousness. This statement is not for the purpose of individual salvation but for the purpose of total salvation. When I think about this, I cannot help but worry that the path I have walked in my life has been sorrowful, but the path ahead is even more serious and tense.  
We know that to lead us forward, sometimes you must walk a path of tears and struggle with a sad situation. Moreover, have compassion for their sorrowful positions, so that the place where they serve you can become a foundation for the gospel, and let new historical creations unfold in that place. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
I have not forgotten the command you gave me when I pioneered the sorrowful valley path in prison. Although decades have passed, I know that the emotional connection from that time has not yet conquered time and space. If you have sons and daughters who love me, please love them in my place, and if there is a foundation of merit that I have established, please share it with this nation and the world.  
So that they may receive the grace of liberation and become the harbingers of tomorrow's hope, may they remain as a group that returns glory and joy to your presence, and may they be allowed to grow in number. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
On the first day of the lunar new year in 1970, as we welcomed a new morning, I have abundantly fulfilled the wishes I set for 1970. Father, how much have you worked? The one who can be praised is not the teacher of the Unification Church. You are the sorrowful Father, the lonely Father, the pitiful Father. You still bear the sorrowful heart that has not washed away the bloodstains of your wounds, yet you have forgotten yourself and come out seeking the sons and daughters who must perish for the sake of the will.  
We know that we must spend the remaining 1970 in holiness.  
There have been many international events during this time. You have protected us during the periods we were worried about, and through such events, we thank you for allowing us to align the posture of the nation with a single goal.  
When I think of the new providence in Asia that can align with heavenly fortune, I know that all of this is your grace, and I thank you.  
Although the Unification Church may seem to lack blessings and be lonely and pitiful, I realize that there is a promise for the future and hope connected behind it, so please do not let us become pitiful ones who suffer the sorrow of being left behind.  
Just as I have gritted my teeth and opened my eyes wide to walk this path, may these also grit their teeth and open their eyes wide to inherit the standard of hope for tomorrow. Father, please drive them with a whip, more coldly and harshly than with love.  
May they be equipped with the victorious authority that can bring you joy and stand in the position to receive the second and third liberation. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Until now, you have held on to the Unification Church and this son standing here. Thank you for your hard work. I cannot fathom your great grace.  
Now, as we pass 1970 and enter 1971, we must prepare to look at the joyful world from a busy position and equip ourselves with what we must have. We must have a time to serve you with filial piety, so we must die.
We must prepare the sanctuary we need by overcoming difficulties and hardships, and we must also prepare the homes we need, as well as the educational institutions and training centers we require.

We are grateful for the abundant love of the Father, who has allowed us to make every effort centered around the year 1970. Receiving your unimaginable blessings, we are infinitely thankful.

I have not relied on people to manage this work. I started this work relying on you, and when I think about how I have borne fruit relying on you, I cannot help but thank you. I feel sorrowful for the responsibility of not being able to establish the conditions for the unification groups to join together and give thanks with you, but I earnestly ask for your forgiveness, as I have made promises to leave at least some conditions.

In the joyful 1970s, may our flags cover the heavens and the earth, and may we prepare a victorious march that can resonate throughout all of Asia and leave a new message and a new alarm in the hearts of all humanity, allowing us to proceed directly according to the purpose you commanded and to become sons and daughters who can burn with righteousness. However, I know that even when you feel anger or resentment, you endure and work. Father, please encourage the unification groups. Father, please encourage the daughters who stand on the front lines. I earnestly pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

**Love**
<Summary of the Message> A sacrifice represents the life of that person and embodies their ideology. When purchasing items to be offered as sacrifices, do not haggle; give a little more. The same applies when buying ceremonial garments.

Sad things must be completely handed over to Satan, and joyful things must be completely taken from Satan and offered to God. Generally, the power of action diminishes as it progresses. However, love is not like that. Once love is given, it returns even greater. From there, heaven opens up, and eternal life emerges. Eternal life can only come from love.

Life is the action of the power necessary to establish a relationship between the subject and object that can receive love.

The son of faith comes to sacrifice his life in proportion to the love of his faithful parents.

To restore, God and Adam must become one in love. Then, by becoming one with the archangel in love, we can return to the Garden of Eden.

The issue of rulers and the ruled can only be resolved through the bond of wealth.

Jesus redeemed the loss of his family through tribal restoration.

**On Nurturing Members**
<Summary of the Message> At the same time as delivering the word, there is a responsibility to nurture people. We must love them. We must nurture living beings.

The problem is how to teach God correctly. We must create the second creation, that is, the sons and daughters of God. After teaching God, we must show God. That is, we must show God's life, and the standard for that is the heart of the parents.

In showing God's life, you must concretely become a model in your personal life. And when you stand on the altar, you must only speak God's word. To do this, you must become a vessel of God's public spirit.

The entire nation must be armed with the ideology of our Unification Church.

**Starting the Year 1971**
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Today is the day we welcome the new year of 1971, and at the same time, it is the day we celebrate the third anniversary of God's Day, which we observe as a precious holiday. To commemorate this day, the members have gathered here, so please bless them. I earnestly hope that your glory may be with us.

As we think about the bloody struggles your children have gone through to find your family, your church, and your nation on the long road of restoration, it is heartbreaking to realize that the mistakes of our ancestors have led to such a sorrowful historical journey... That path was one of sorrow that no one knew. How much have you struggled to take responsibility and guide your ignorant children? How much effort have you put into bringing the ignorant people and humanity into the world of your will?

When we look at the democratic world, there are heavenly nations that have emerged at the end of paying the price of blood centered around Christianity, while there is also a world of opposition, and now the inside and outside have become a divided reality, where the heart governs the body, and we realize that the time is coming when you will govern the created world.

When we face the current situation where the democratic world has lost its subjectivity, all people do not know the path they should take and are groaning in sorrow, pain, and despair. Father, please show them the way in light of this tragic situation. We know that you have a will to realize your hopeful sons and daughters, families, churches, nations, and states through them.

There have been countless religions for this purpose, but we thank you for your hard work in leading us through the decisive path centered on the Unification Church. You have stood before us in the process of the Unification Church's struggles, fulfilling the mission of a pioneer, and we know how much you have worried about your sons and daughters being harmed while confronting Satan on the front lines of battle. Because of such protection and concern, you have allowed us to establish the connection of the True Parents on this earth today and to establish the connection of true families. We are also truly grateful for your efforts in bringing us to the victorious stage where we can resolve the grievances that Jesus could not resolve on behalf of the church and the nation.

Father, on this morning of God's Day, may you embrace the year 1971. We know that this year is an important year that will never come again in history. The heavenly family must be newly dedicated before you. All the apostles in the spirit world centered on Jesus and our ancestors within the spiritual Israel world have set this day as a day of reunion through the humanity of this earth to achieve the restoration of all things, so I earnestly hope and wish that you may receive this day as holy.

Centered on the heavenly family, the spiritual families representing the spirit world and the families of the earth must become one, the spiritual tribes and the earthly tribes must become one, the spiritual nations and the earthly nations must become one, and the spiritual countries and the earthly countries must become one to build the victorious unified kingdom centered on you. This is your wish, our wish, and the wish of the spirit world. Therefore, we know that this is a significant turning point in world history to restore the original state where Adam and Eve were separated from you and the archangel.

For this reason, we must unite and move forward under the holy goal of 'securing a foundation for unification' this year.

Centered on your nation, we must unite individuals, families, tribes, and nations so that this country can raise the flag of victory before you and establish the authority of a sovereign nation throughout the world. This is the mission of our time that is approaching us, so I earnestly hope and wish that you may bless us holy.

Now, we must not serve you conceptually but must serve you in reality, and we must not serve the hopeful families conceptually but must pour out all our sincerity and love to serve you in reality, knowing that we have the tremendous fact of having a day to prepare for victory on this earth.

Father, may you deepen today's blessing and make it a day when we can present the conditions for the restoration of all people, and may it be a day of victory that can resolve the groans of all nations, I earnestly hope and wish.

Here, the humble children gather their insufficient sincerity and bow their heads before you, and I earnestly hope that you may come and bless them. The children gathered here represent thirty million people of the nation and countless tribes. Even though this place may be limited, when we realize that it is the place where you look upon as the center of all and the center of love, we know that where your heart is, your life flourishes, and your love also flourishes. May you determine this precious value and let your heart dwell among the thirty million people of South Korea. May your love be with us, and may the connection of your life spread forth.

Please allow this currently divided nation of the North and South to fulfill the origin of unification. We know that the time is approaching when you will remove those opposing forces according to your will, so may the workers of unification in South Korea prepare the altar and engage in the fight to discern Satan, becoming one with the holy altar. We must recognize that the Unification Church must take on the priestly responsibility to offer this nation as a sacrifice to be presented before you.

May you unify the spirit world and the Unification Church. Please help us to discern the spiritual Satan and the earthly Satan, so that we can establish a foundation of discernment in the spiritual and physical worlds. Thus, we must offer the whole as a holy sacrifice before you centered on the purpose of unification. For this, there must be men and women in the family, and there must be internal and external families based on the expectation of children. Centered on such families, such churches, and such nations, the representative form has now been established here, so Father, please receive it. Based on this, may you extend your power, and I earnestly hope and wish that it may be fulfilled within your will.

Until now, the Unification Church has walked the path of persecution with tearful steps, but as I recall the sad days when you could not deal with them because you were on our side, I realize that the time has come for you to stand by us and remove evil centered around the beginning of 1971. Until now, we have gone through the path of restoration by striking good sons and daughters, but we now understand that it is time to strike evil and bring about restoration.

Now is the time when the era is changing and the world is changing. We know that 1971 must be set as a time to restore and remove evil, so may you extend the glorious authority of the Father upon this earth from this day, which marks the third anniversary of God's Day.

Please subdue those who do not know you and consider themselves high. Please subdue those who disregard your sovereignty and consider themselves high. Thus, may the day come soon when only you can govern, and your children can serve you in your nation and praise your glory.

May the unification groups live in such a way, and may the leaders who move the unification church be able to live in this manner.

Those who elevate themselves are exceedingly foolish, and being intoxicated by the position of self is a path that binds oneself. We now ask that you teach us your strategy so that we may live according to all public paths and die according to public connections, becoming sons and daughters who are worthy of inheriting the heavenly legacy for ten thousand generations. Father! We thank you for the blessing of teaching us various contents on this holy day.

We earnestly hope and wish that, knowing this, we can become sons and daughters who can be used by you as offerings of holy victory and offerings of life. We pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
          Selected Words of Rev. Sun Myung Moon <Volume 37>
